# diś

_PWG article — 49 sub-card(s), 375 sense(s) · RU 317/375 · EN 308/375_

## diś

`di_s~~h0_00_pwg00`


**headnote)** *diś*¦, *dideṣṭi* und *diśati* (spätere Form, [DHĀTUP. 28,3](https://www.sanskrit-lexicon.uni-koeln.de/scans/csl-westergaard/disp/index.php?section=28)); *pradiśyati* [MBH. 1,6472](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.6472); *dideśa; dekṣyati, deṣṭā* Kār. [5](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.5) aus [SIDDH. K.] zu [P. 7,2,10](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/7/2/10); *adikṣat* [P. 3,1,45](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/1/45); med. selten, obgleich im [DHĀTUP.] als gleichberechtigt angegeben; *adiṣṭa* ved.; *diṣṭa* .

- **RU:** *diś*¦, *dideṣṭi* и *diśati* (более поздняя форма, [DHĀTUP. 28,3](https://www.sanskrit-lexicon.uni-koeln.de/scans/csl-westergaard/disp/index.php?section=28)); *pradiśyati* [MBH. 1,6472](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.6472); *dideśa; dekṣyati, deṣṭā* Kār. [5](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.5) из [SIDDH. K.] к [P. 7,2,10](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/7/2/10); *adikṣat* [P. 3,1,45](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/1/45); med. редко, хотя в [DHĀTUP.] указывается как равноправная; *adiṣṭa* ved.; *diṣṭa* .
- **EN:** *diś*¦, *dideṣṭi* and *diśati* (later form,
[DHĀTUP. 28,3](https://www.sanskrit-lexicon.uni-koeln.de/scans/csl-westergaard/disp/index.php?section=28)); *pradiśyati*
[MBH. 1,6472](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.6472); *dideśa; dekṣyati, deṣṭā* Kār.
[5](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.5) from [SIDDH. K.] to [P. 7,2,10](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/7/2/10); *adikṣat*
[P. 3,1,45](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/3/1/45); med. rare, although given
in [DHĀTUP.] as equally valid; *adiṣṭa* ved.; *diṣṭa* .

**1)** 1) zeigen, vorweisen, vorführen (einen Zeugen): *sākṣiṇaḥ santi metyuktvā* (d. i. *ma ityu˚) diśetyukto diśenna yaḥ* [M. 8,57.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,57) [52.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,52) [53.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,53)

- **RU:** 1) показывать, предъявлять, представлять (свидетеля): *sākṣiṇaḥ santi metyuktvā* (d. i. *ma ityu˚) diśetyukto diśenna yaḥ* [M. 8,57.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,57) [52.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,52) [53.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,53)
- **EN:** 1) to show, point out, produce, exhibit (a witness): *sākṣiṇaḥ santi metyuktvā* (d. i. *ma ityu˚) diśetyukto diśenna yaḥ*
[M. 8,57.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,57) [52.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,52) [53.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,53)

**4)** — 4) mit einem infin. heissen: *smartuṃ diśanti na divaḥ* heissen Einen des Himmels nicht gedenken [KIR. 5,28.]

**1)** Etwas zeigen, anweisen: *deśayanniva panthānam*

[SADDH. P. 4,4,b.] *bhagavato dharmaṃ deśayamānasya* 5, a. anzeigen so v. a. bekennen, beichten: *atyayamatyayato deśaya*
[BURN. Intr. 299.]
- **EN:** to show, indicate something: *deśayanniva panthānam*
[R. 3,78,13.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?3,78,13)
[MBH. 6,121.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?6.121) (to direct, instruct), thus v. a. (to teach, communicate): *yadāpi bhagavāndharmaṃ deśayati*
[SADDH. P. 4,4,b.] *bhagavato dharmaṃ deśayamānasya* 5, a. to indicate, declare, thus v. a. (to confess, avow): *atyayamatyayato deśaya*
[BURN. Intr. 299.]

**1)** — *ati*
 1) hinüberweisen, übertragen
[ŚAT. BR. 4,3,4,32.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?4,3,4,32) [14,1,1,32.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shatapathabr/app1?14,1,1,32)
[KĀTY. ŚR. 25,2,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/katyasr/app1?25,2,4)
[ĀŚV. ŚR. 9,1.] Häufig bei den Grammatikern das pass.: *puṃvadbhāvenāntaratamaḥ puṃśabdo 'tidiśyate* durch die Gleichsetzung mit der masculinen Form wird die zunächststehende masculine Form als auch für jene (die weibliche Form) geltend angenommen
[KĀŚ.] zu [P. 1,1,50.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/1/50) *vāmarathasya kaṇvādivatsvaravarjam .. lugādikamatidiśyate* mit dem Worte *vāmaratha* geht dasselbe vor was mit *kaṇva* u. s. w. mit Ausnahme des Tones; (d. h.) *luk* u. s. w. wird auf jenes übertragen, ausgedehnt, auch von diesem gilt *luk* u. s. w.
[P. 4,1,151](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/4/1/151), Vārtt. nebst Scholien.

ŚR. 9,1.] Frequently in the grammarians the pass.: *puṃvadbhāvenāntaratamaḥ puṃśabdo 'tidiśyate* by equating it with the masculine form, the nearest preceding masculine form is taken as valid also for that (the feminine form) too [KĀŚ.] on [P. 1,1,50.](https://ashtadhyayi.com/sutraani/1/1/50) *vāmarathasya kaṇvādivatsvaravarjam .. lugādikamatidiśyate* with the word *vāmaratha* the same applies as with *kaṇva* u. s. w., except for the accent; (d. h.) *luk* u. s. w. is transferred, extended to that, the same also holds of this *luk* u. s. w. ## upādiś

`di_s~~h0_15_up_a`


**1)** — *upā*
 1) anweisen, zuweisen: (Drupada spricht zu Yudhiṣṭhira) *bhavānvā vidhivatpāṇiṃ gṛhṇātu duhiturmama . yasya vā manyase vīra tasya kṛṣṇāmupādiśa*
[MBH. 1,7239.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.7239)

- **RU:** — *upā*
 1) указывать, назначать: (Drupada говорит Yudhiṣṭhira) *bhavānvā vidhivatpāṇiṃ gṛhṇātu duhiturmama . yasya vā manyase vīra tasya kṛṣṇāmupādiśa*
[MBH. 1,7239.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.7239)
- **EN:** — *upā*
 1) to instruct, to assign: (Drupada speaks to Yudhiṣṭhira) *bhavānvā vidhivatpāṇiṃ gṛhṇātu duhiturmama . yasya vā manyase vīra tasya kṛṣṇāmupādiśa*
[MBH. 1,7239.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.7239)
  <sub>DCS 4 · attested</sub>

**2)** — 2) anzeigen, mittheilen, verkünden: *iti rājña upadiśya viprā jātakakovidāḥ*
[BHĀG. P. 1,12,29.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?1,12,29)

- **RU:** — 2) указывать, сообщать, возвещать: *iti rājña upadiśya viprā jātakakovidāḥ*
[BHĀG. P. 1,12,29.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?1,12,29)
- **EN:** — 2) to indicate, communicate, proclaim: *iti rājña upadiśya viprā jātakakovidāḥ*
[BHĀG. P. 1,12,29.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?1,12,29)
  <sub>DCS 4 · attested</sub>

**3)** — 3) Etwas vorschreiben oder Jmd anweisen, einen Befehl ertheilen: *tapasyupadiṣṭa* (kann loc. und nom. _m._ sein) *ivādadhe manaḥ*
[BHĀG. P. 2,9,7.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?2,9,7)

- **RU:** — 3) предписывать что-л. или давать указание кому-л., отдавать приказ: *tapasyupadiṣṭa* (может быть loc. и nom. _m._) *ivādadhe manaḥ*
[BHĀG. P. 2,9,7.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?2,9,7)
- **EN:** — 3) to prescribe something or to instruct someone, to issue a command: *tapasyupadiṣṭa* (can be loc. and nom. _m._) *ivādadhe manaḥ*
[BHĀG. P. 2,9,7.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?2,9,7)
  <sub>DCS 4 · attested</sub>

 1) eine Anweisung geben, vorschreiben, anempfehlen: *pratyādiṣṭaṃ *

* mayā tatra tvayi karmavimohite*

* mayā tatra tvayi karmavimohite*
[BHĀG. P. 2,9,22.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?2,9,22) *atha vā vai paraguṇāṃ buddhiṃ pratyādiśanti naḥ*

- **EN:** — *pratyā*
 1) to give an instruction, prescribe, recommend: *pratyādiṣṭaṃ *

* mayā tatra tvayi karmavimohite*

## samādiś

`di_s~~h0_19_sam_a`


**1)** — *samā*

[MBH. 4,1024.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?4.1024)

[KATHĀS. 2,17.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?2,17) *gavāṃ śatasahasraṃ hi brāhmaṇebhyo narādhipaḥ . ekaikaśo dadau rājā putrānuddiśya dharmataḥ ..* in the name of the sons
[R. 1,72,22](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?1,72,22) (GORR. [74,28](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?1,74,28)). *rāmaścopetya vijñāpyo māmuddiśya sagauravam* from me, in my name
[R. GORR. 1,80,21.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?1,80,21) *vacasi bhavati saṃtyāgamuddiśya vārttā śrutimukharamukhānāṃ kevalaṃ paṇḍitānām* thus v. a. the practice of renunciation
[BHARTṚ. 1,56.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhartrhari/app2?1,56) With obj. to be supplied: *sālaṃkārāngajānaśvānkanyāścaiva varastriyaḥ . uddiśyoddiśya sarvebhyo dadau* according to the sense thus v. a. to this one, to that one
[MBH. 15,414.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?15.414)
  <sub>DCS 567 · attested</sub>

[YĀJÑ. 1,250](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/yajnavalkya/app1?1,250)).

**2)** — 2) absol. *samuddiśya* mit Hinweisung auf (acc.) so v. a. auf, gegen: *na ripūnvai samuddiśya vimuñcanti narāḥ śarān*

[MBH. 4,435.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?4.435) *adyaiva ca tvayā rāma gantavyaṃ vacanātpituḥ . vanavāsaṃ samuddiśya nava varṣāṇi pañca ca ..* um im Walde 14 Jahre zu leben

## pratyupadiś

`di_s~~h0_24_pratyupa`


**1)** — *pratyupa*
 1) einzeln auseinandersetzen: *(karma) vyādhiṃ prati pratyupadekṣyāmaḥ*
[SUŚR. 1,14,17.]

- **RU:** — *pratyupa*
 1) подробно излагать, разъяснять по отдельности: *(karma) vyādhiṃ prati pratyupadekṣyāmaḥ*
[SUŚR. 1,14,17.]
- **EN:** — *pratyupa*
 1) to expound singly, one by one: *(karma) vyādhiṃ prati pratyupadekṣyāmaḥ*
[SUŚR. 1,14,17.]
  <sub>DCS 1 · attested</sub>

**2)** — 2) Etwas Jmd zurücklehren: *yadyatprayogaviṣaye bhāvikamupadiśyate mayā tasyai . tattadviśeṣakaraṇātpratyupadiśatīva me bālā ..*
[MĀLAV. 5.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/malavikagni/app1?5)

- **RU:** — 2) обучать кого-л. чему-л. в ответ, преподавать в качестве обратного наставления: *yadyatprayogaviṣaye bhāvikamupadiśyate mayā tasyai . tattadviśeṣakaraṇātpratyupadiśatīva me bālā ..*
[MĀLAV. 5.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/malavikagni/app1?5)
- **EN:** — 2) to teach something back to someone: *yadyatprayogaviṣaye bhāvikamupadiśyate mayā tasyai . tattadviśeṣakaraṇātpratyupadiśatīva me bālā ..*
[MĀLAV. 5.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/malavikagni/app1?5)
  <sub>DCS 1 · attested</sub>

- **RU:** — Vgl. *pratyupadeśa* .
- **EN:** — Vgl. *pratyupadeśa* .

## samupadiś

`di_s~~h0_25_samupa`


**1)** — *samupa* zeigen, hinweisen auf: *kimarthaṃ vidarbhāṇāṃ panthāḥ samupadiśyate*

[MBH. 3,2328.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.2328) zeigen so v. a. zuweisen, zukommen lassen: *anena kṛtakṛtyo 'smi yanmāṃ sa puruṣeśvaraḥ — mṛtyuṃ samupadekṣyati*
[R. 3,45,18.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?3,45,18)

- **RU:** — *samupa* указывать, показывать на: *kimarthaṃ vidarbhāṇāṃ panthāḥ samupadiśyate*

[MBH. 3,2328.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.2328) показывать, так v. a. назначать, предоставлять: *anena kṛtakṛtyo 'smi yanmāṃ sa puruṣeśvaraḥ — mṛtyuṃ samupadekṣyati*
[R. 3,45,18.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?3,45,18)
- **EN:** — *samupa* to show, point to: *kimarthaṃ vidarbhāṇāṃ panthāḥ samupadiśyate*

[MBH. 3,2328.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.2328) to show, hence v. a. to assign, allot to: *anena kṛtakṛtyo 'smi yanmāṃ sa puruṣeśvaraḥ — mṛtyuṃ samupadekṣyati*
[R. 3,45,18.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanagorr/?3,45,18)
  <sub>DCS 9 · attested</sub>

## diś

`di_s~~h0_zz_pw02`


**1)** **2.** *diś*¦ _f._
— 1〉 Richtung, Himmelsrichtung, Himmelsgegend. *diśi diśi* allerwärts, nach allen Richtungen hin [172,8](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?172). Pl. so v. a. alle Himmelsgegenden und die ganze Welt ([LA. 89,13]). Von einem Erschrockenen heisst es, dass er nach allen Himmelsgegenden aussehe [320,14](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?320). *diśo 'ntāt* Es werden 4,5,6,7,8,9 ([SUPARṆ. 28,3]) und 10 Himmelsrichtungen angenommen. *etā daśa diśaḥ* elliptisch so v. a. alle Wege stehen dir offen, gehe wohin dir beliebt. *diśāṃ vrataṃ daśānugānam* Name eines Sāman.
- **EN:** **2.** *diś* _f._ — 1) direction, cardinal point, quarter of the sky. *diśi diśi* everywhere, in all directions [172,8](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?172). Pl. thus v. a. all the quarters of the sky and the whole world ([LA. 89,13]). Of a frightened person it is said that he looks about in all directions [320,14](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?320). *diśo 'ntāt* 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 9 ([SUPARṆ. 28,3]) and 10 cardinal points are assumed. *etā daśa diśaḥ* elliptically thus v. a. all roads lie open to you, go wherever you please. *diśāṃ vrataṃ daśānugānam* name of a Sāman.

**2)** — 2〉 Bez. der Zahl zehn.
- **EN:** — 2) Bez. of the number ten.

**3)** — 3〉 Gegend, Ort [113,32](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?113).
- **EN:** — 3) region, place [113,32](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?113).

**4)** — 4〉 Raum (neben *kāla* Zeit) [KAP. 2,12].
- **EN:** — 4) space (alongside *kāla* time) [KAP. 2,12].

**5)** — 5〉 die Fremde.
- **EN:** — 5) foreign land, abroad.

**6)** — 6〉 Andeutung, Hinweis, Anweisung, Beispiel.
- **EN:** — 6) hint, indication, instruction, example.

**7)** — 7〉 Art und Weise.
- **EN:** — 7) manner, way.

**8)** — 8〉 die Spur eines Bisses.
- **EN:** — 8) the mark of a bite.

**9)** — 9〉 N. pr.
— a〉 eines Flusses.
— b〉 Pl. = *diśa* 2〉b〉 [VP. 1,8,9].
- **EN:** — 9) N. pr. — a) of a river. — b) Pl. = *diśa* 2)b) [VP. 1,8,9].

**1)** **3.** *√*diś*¦ volksthümlich = *darś* sehen [MAHĀBH. (K.) 259,14].
- **EN:** 3. *√*diś* popularly = *darś* to see [MAHĀBH. (K.) 259,14].

**1)** **1.** √*diś*¦ mit *samā* Z. 3, lies [231,16].
- **EN:** 1. √*diś* with *samā* l. 3, read [231,16].

**1)** **1.** √*diś*¦ mit *anvā* III. Jmd (Acc.) befehlen [JĀTAKAM. 20]. Befehl geben [22].
- **EN:** 1. √*diś* with *anvā* III. to command someone (Acc.) [JĀTAKAM. 20]; to give an order [22].

**2)** — Mit *samā* III. 3.
- **EN:** — With *samā* III. 3.

**3)** — Mit *ud* auch abweisen [R. ed. Bomb. 3,46,35](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanabom/app1/?3,46,35).
- **EN:** — With *ud* also to turn away, repel [R. ed. Bomb. 3,46,35](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanabom/app1/?3,46,35).

**4)** — Mit *sam* III. Abschied nehmen von (Acc.) [DIVYĀVAD. 446,25].
- **EN:** — With *sam* III. to take leave of (Acc.) [DIVYĀVAD. 446,25].

**1)** **2.** √*diś*¦ III. 1〉 *diśo digbhyaḥ* in allen Richtungen [DIVYĀVAD. 163,24].
- **EN:** 2. √*diś* III. 1) *diśo digbhyaḥ* in all directions [DIVYĀVAD. 163,24].
